99:["$","ul","ul-8",{"children":["\n",["$","li","li-0",{"children":["Multi stage algorithm for edge detection: 多阶段边缘检测算法\n",["$","ul","ul-0",{"children":["\n",["$","li","li-0",{"children":"Step 1: Noise reduction - typically uses Gaussian (but any denoising can be used) 降噪-通常使用高斯(但也可以使用任何降噪)"}],"\n",["$","li","li-1",{"children":"Step 2: Gradient calculation - detect edges, typically along 4 directions, horizontal, vertical, and two diagonals. (e.g. use Sobel) 梯度计算-检测边缘，通常沿 4 个方向，水平，垂直和两个对角线。\n(如使用 Sobel)"}],"\n",["$","li","li-2",{"children":"Step 3: Non-maximum suppression - thin out edges by finding pixels with max value in the edge direction.  非最大抑制-通过在边缘方向上找到最大值像素来减少边缘。"}],"\n",["$","li","li-3",{"children":"Step 4: Double threshold - determines potential edges by double thresholding to obtain strong, weak and irrelevant pixels for edges. 双阈值-通过双阈值确定潜在的边缘，获得边缘的强、弱和无关像素。"}],"\n",["$","li","li-4",{"children":"Step 5: Edge tracking by hysteresis - covert weak edge pixels to strong based on neighboring pixels. 边缘跟踪的迟滞-隐藏弱边缘像素到强基于邻近像素。"}],"\n"]}],"\n"]}],"\n"]}]
